Action.c(76):     ** define and instantiate validation objects\n

Action.c(76):     **\n

Action.c(76):     **   eltType: element type (we have to create this since IE3\n
Action.c(76):     **       doesn't support the type property for for elements)\n
Action.c(76):     **     text\n
Action.c(76):     **     textarea\n

Action.c(76):     **     select\n
Action.c(76):     **\n

Action.c(76):     **     isText(str)\n

Action.c(76):     **     isRadio(formObj)\n
Action.c(76):     **     isCheck(formObj, form, [index of first checkbox in group],\n

Action.c(76):       this.eltType = eltType;\n

Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(76):     ** create a new object for each form element you need to validate\n

Action.c(76):     ** var phoneNum = new validation('phone number', 'phoneNum', 'text', 'isPhoneNum(str)', 'x
Action.c(76):     xx-xxx-xxxx');\n

Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(76):     ** these functions validate the string or form object passed in,\n
Action.c(76):     ** and return true or false based on whether the test succeeds or fails\n
Action.c(76):     **\n
Action.c(76):     ** validate existence of input\n
Action.c(76):     **   isText(str): verifies text input or textarea is not empty\n
Action.c(76):     **   isSelect(formObj): verifies item from a select menu is chosen\n
Action.c(76):     **   isRadio(formObj): verifies one of a group of radio buttons is chosen\n
Action.c(76):     **   isCheck(formObj, form, [begin], [num]): verifies at least one\n
Action.c(76):     **       of a group of checkboxes is checked\n
Action.c(76):     **     for [begin], fill in the index number in the elements array\n

Action.c(76):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(76):     ** these functions validate the string or form object passed in,\n
Action.c(76):     ** and return true or false based on whether the test succeeds or fails\n
Action.c(76):     **\n
Action.c(76):     ** validate existence of input\n
Action.c(76):     **   isText(str): verifies text input or textarea is not empty\n
Action.c(76):     **   isSelect(formObj): verifies item from a select menu is chosen\n
Action.c(76):     **   isRadio(formObj): verifies one of a group of radio buttons is chosen\n
Action.c(76):     **   isCheck(formObj, form, [begin], [num]): verifies at least one\n
Action.c(76):     **       of a group of checkboxes is checked\n
Action.c(76):     **     for [begin], fill in the index number in the elements array\n
Action.c(76):     **         of the first checkbox (remember to start counting from zero)\n
Action.c(76):     **     for [num], fill in the number of checkboxes in the group\n
Action.c(76):     **\n
Action.c(76):     ** validate text in text input or textarea matches pattern\n
Action.c(76):     **   isEmail(str): verifies email address (contains "@" and ".")\n
Action.c(76):     **   isState(str): verifies U.S. State Code\n
Action.c(76):     **   isZipCode(str): verifies zip code of form xxxxx or xxxxx-xxxx\n
Action.c(76):     **   isPhoneNum(str): verifies phone number of form xxx-xxx-xxxx\n
Action.c(76):     **   isDate(str): verifies date of form mm/dd/yyyy\n
Action.c(76):     ***************************************************************/\n
Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     function isText(str) {\n
Action.c(76):       return (str != "");\n
Action.c(76):     }\n
Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     function isSelect(formObj) {\n
Action.c(76):       return (formObj.selectedIndex != 0);\n
Action.c(76):     }\n
Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     function isRadio(formObj) {\n
Action.c(76):       for (j=0; j<formObj.length; j++) {\n
Action.c(76):         if (formObj[j].checked) {\n
Action.c(76):           return true;\n
Action.c(76):         }\n
Action.c(76):       }\n
Action.c(76):       return false;\n
Action.c(76):     }\n
Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     function isCheck(formObj, form, begin, num) {\n
Action.c(76):       for (j=begin; j<begin+num; j++) {\n
Action.c(76):         if (form.elements[j].checked) {\n
Action.c(76):           return true;\n
Action.c(76):         }\n
Action.c(76):       }\n
Action.c(76):       return false;\n
Action.c(76):     }\n

Action.c(76):     ** these functions validate the string or form object passed in,\n
Action.c(76):     ** and return true or false based on whether the test succeeds or fails\n
Action.c(76):     **\n
Action.c(76):     ** validate existence of input\n
Action.c(76):     **   isText(str): verifies text input or textarea is not empty\n
Action.c(76):     **   isSelect(formObj): verifies item from a select menu is chosen\n
Action.c(76):     **   isRadio(formObj): verifies one of a group of radio buttons is chosen\n
Action.c(76):     **   isCheck(formObj, form, [begin], [num]): verifies at least one\n
Action.c(76):     **       of a group of checkboxes is checked\n
Action.c(76):     **     for [begin], fill in the index number in the elements array\n
Action.c(76):     **         of the first checkbox (remember to start counting from zero)\n
Action.c(76):     **     for [num], fill in the number of checkboxes in the group\n
Action.c(76):     **\n
Action.c(76):     ** validate text in text input or textarea matches pattern\n
Action.c(76):     **   isEmail(str): verifies email address (contains "@" and ".")\n
Action.c(76):     **   isState(str): verifies U.S. State Code\n
Action.c(76):     **   isZipCode(str): verifies zip code of form xxxxx or xxxxx-xxxx\n
Action.c(76):     **   isPhoneNum(str): verifies phone number of form xxx-xxx-xxxx\n
Action.c(76):     **   isDate(str): verifies date of form mm/dd/yyyy\n
Action.c(76):     ***************************************************************/\n
Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     function isText(str) {\n
Action.c(76):       return (str != "");\n
Action.c(76):     }\n
Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     function isSelect(formObj) {\n
Action.c(76):       return (formObj.selectedIndex != 0);\n
Action.c(76):     }\n
Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     function isRadio(formObj) {\n
Action.c(76):       for (j=0; j<formObj.length; j++) {\n
Action.c(76):         if (formObj[j].checked) {\n
Action.c(76):           return true;\n
Action.c(76):         }\n
Action.c(76):       }\n
Action.c(76):       return false;\n
Action.c(76):     }\n
Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     function isCheck(formObj, form, begin, num) {\n
Action.c(76):       for (j=begin; j<begin+num; j++) {\n
Action.c(76):         if (form.elements[j].checked) {\n
Action.c(76):           return true;\n
Action.c(76):         }\n
Action.c(76):       }\n
Action.c(76):       return false;\n
Action.c(76):     }\n
Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     function isEmail(str) {\n
Action.c(76):       return ((str != "") && (str.indexOf("@") != -1) && (str.indexOf(".") != -1));\n
Action.c(76):     }\n
Action.c(76):     \n
Action.c(76):     function isState(str) {\n

Action.c(76):       for (j=0; j<formObj.length; j++) {\n
Action.c(76):         if (formObj[j].checked) {\n
Action.c(76):           return true;\n
Action.c(76):         }\n
Action.c(76):       }\n
Action.c(76):       return false;\n
Action.c(76):     }\n
Action.c(76):     \n

Action.c(76):           return true;\n
Action.c(76):         }\n
Action.c(76):       }\n
Action.c(76):       return false;\n
Action.c(76):     }\n

Action.c(76):     function isZipCode(str) {\n
Action.c(76):       var l = str.length;\n
Action.c(76):       if ((l != 5) && (l != 10)) { return false }\n
